creature_p17 
[OBJECT:CREATURE]
list of creatures
HELLACOPTER a flaming thieving flying metal creature
TRUCK a metal wagon
GEMINI a two bodied creature from hell
SALAMANDER a fire-breathing lizard. somehow requires leather. how did it get skin?
VULCAN an unemotional humanoid
CAPITALIST a greedy stubborn dwarvenoid.
SLAVE a slave that evil creatures can use
ARMOKIAN:they want one thing... your blood.
SUPER_HERO:some have powers, some of whom are good, and some of whom are evil.
LIGHT_RIDER the commander of the light armies.
SHADOW_SEEKER a nocturnal civ koboldoid.
RABBIT:the killer rabbit. holy hand grenades not implemented
KARP kobolds combined with carp. keep your aquifers litter free
KRAKEN:release the kraken! not a megabeast
POKEBALL a pokeball healing creature
GALVANTULA:giant cave spider. except it's a pokemon.
PIKACHU a pikachu, my namesake. this creature has lightning bolts and crunches you.
MILTANK a cow pokemon. not much to see here
MEOWTH a cat that occasionally makes free golden coins.
PURRLOIN:like meowth, but evil
GENGAR a gremlin named gengar
EEVEE:the pokemon eevee. can evolve into other pokemon. in addition to the other advantages of evolving, evolved eevees can't be transformed into a werebeast or anything similar
PIGTAIL:a horrific sock puppet.
CANNON:various immobile cannons
BEAVER:a beaver. can dam you for all eternity
DAM:
PHASE_SPIDER:phase spiders can hide, and will use special webbing to escape.
LEVIATHON:a large serpent in the cavern. meant to have deadly gas, but it doesn't seem to work.
DARK_KNIGHT:dark knight from Monty Python and the Holy Grail. will bite your limbs off.
SLIME:slimy slimy sliming slime.
PEGASUS:Pegasus, the winged horse. Relays his messages by Morse.
WOOD_IMP:mischevious forest imp. 
ROGEODO:10 headed creaure with two hands on each head. named "many-head"
SUCCUBUS:comes from the HFS, and seduces males into becoming an incubus
EATEN:an instakill creature
HEAL:a creature for transformation healing
GHOUL:a radioactive monster. infectious.
PHANTOM:an unhittable spirit. may be harmed by special priests(priests not implimented)
NECROBEE:the hives create bees. the bees kill. the hives use corpses to make new bees.
BASE_BULBORB:the creature from Pikmin. this is the base of all other bulborbs. two other bulborbs.
WALLMASTER:wallmasters, from Legend of Zelda. No longer takes you to any entrance, except the entrance to hell.
FLICKY:a small blue bird.
CRABBY:small crab-like robot.
